<script type="text/javascript">
    var StatusReadyValidator = function(){};
    StatusReadyValidator.prototype.status = {
        ads: {
            multiRun: false,
            status: {
                cmp: false,
                adhesion: false,
                adManager: false,
            },
            callback: [],
        }
    };
    StatusReadyValidator.prototype.statusRegister = function(cat, sec, bool, multiRun) {
        var category = this.status[cat];
        if (typeof category !== "object") {
            category = this.status[cat] = {
                status: {},
                callback: [],
                multiRun: multiRun,
            };
        }
        category.status[sec] = bool;
    }
    StatusReadyValidator.prototype.statusUpdate = function(cat, sec, bool) {
        var category = this.status[cat];
        if (typeof category === "object" && [true, false].indexOf(category.status[sec]) > -1) {
            category.status[sec] = bool;
            if (this.statusValidate(cat)) {
                this.runCallback(cat);
            }
        }
    };
    StatusReadyValidator.prototype.statusValidate = function(cat) {
        var category = this.status[cat];
        if (typeof category === "object" && typeof category.status === "object") {
            var sections = Object.keys(category.status);
            return sections.map(function(secName) {return category.status[secName]}).filter(function(secValue){return secValue === false}).length === 0;
        } else {
            return false;
        }
    }
    StatusReadyValidator.prototype.registerCallback = function(cat, callback) {
        var category = this.status[cat];
        if (typeof category === "object" && Array.isArray(category.callback)) {
            category.callback.push(callback);
        }
    }
    StatusReadyValidator.prototype.runCallback = function(cat) {
        var category = this.status[cat];
        if (typeof category === "object" && Array.isArray(category.callback)) {
            category.callback.forEach(function(callback){callback();})
            !category.multiRun && category.callback.splice(0);
        }
    }
    window.statusReadyValidator = new StatusReadyValidator();
</script>
